[debug] ffmpeg command line: ffmpeg -y -loglevel repeat+info -i file:C:\Temp\yt-dlp\20241112191522.mp4 -map 0 -dn -ignore_unknown -c copy -write_id3v1 1 -metadata "title=Video by her.recipe.journal" -metadata "date=20240825" -metadata "description=Basic Bread Dough Recipe

Ingredients:

        •       8 1/3 cups flour
        •       1 1/4 tablespoons kosher salt
        •       2 teaspoons instant yeast
        •       3 cups water

Instructions:

        1.      Mix the Dry Ingredients:
        •       In a large mixing bowl, combine the flour, kosher salt, and instant yeast. Stir the ingredients together until they are evenly distributed.
        2.      Add Water:
        •       Gradually pour in the 3 cups of water while stirring the mixture. Continue to stir until a dough begins to form.
        3.      Knead the Dough:
        •       Turn the dough onto a lightly floured surface and knead it for about 10 minutes. The dough should become smooth and elastic. If it’s too sticky, you can add a little more flour as needed.
        4.      First Rise:
        •       Place the dough in a lightly greased bowl, cover it with a clean cloth or plastic wrap, and let it rise in a warm place for about 1 to 1.5 hours, or until it has doubled in size or if you have time, leave it for 24hr in the fridge.
        5.      Shape the Dough:
        •       After the dough has risen, punch it down to release the air. Shape the dough as desired, depending on what you’re making (loaf, rolls, pizza, etc.).
        6.      Second Rise:
        •       If you’re making a loaf or rolls, allow the shaped dough to rise again for about 30-60 minutes.
        7.      Bake:
        •       Preheat your oven to 375°F (190°C). Bake the bread for about 25-30 minutes, or until the crust is golden brown and the bread sounds hollow when tapped on the bottom.
        8.      Cool and Serve:
        •       Let the bread cool on a wire rack before slicing and serving.
